Dismissed: copy-btn focus ring "depends on external CSS" (BY DESIGN — focus-motion.css frozen 5.4, DD-15 reuse, proven by the keyboard-vs-mouse Playwright test); tautological substring assertions (intentional static-analysis token contract, behavioral coverage is in Playwright); token-var-only regex weakness (no current raw-px leak; stylelint is the real 5.2 gate); `swapCopyGlyph` hardcoded sprite path (verified identical to `createGlyph`'s `<use href>`, swap proven by test); `data.user || "—"` fallback (defensive default for the exported `renderResumeCard` API); `COPY_FEEDBACK_MS=1000` vs `--motion-copy-feedback` (matches token value; JS mirror avoids fragile `getComputedStyle("1s")→ms` parse); raw `36px` vs `--space-16` (intentional a11y touch-target floor, explicitly whitelisted in the stylelint contract test); greeting suppressed when storage unavailable (deliberate fail-closed — avoids re-greeting every load when persistence is broken).

- **DEF-1 — normalizeCommand preserves interior newlines (multi-line command)** [src/sdlc/dashboard/static/components/resume-card/resume-card.js:18-21] — `String(raw).trim()` + `replace(/\n+$/u,"")` strip only leading/trailing whitespace and trailing newlines; an interior `\n` is copied verbatim, so pasting a multi-line value into a terminal auto-executes up to the newline. **Reason deferred:** the 5.8 synthetic command is single-line and DD-13 mandates only trailing-newline stripping; the real command source (`sdlc status --suggested-next`) is wired in 5.18. **Action on un-defer:** collapse interior newlines (e.g. `replace(/\s*\n\s*/gu," ")`) or reject multi-line commands when real command compute lands. **Owner:** Epic-5 Story 5.18 (real suggested-next). Surfaced by Edge Case Hunter (LOW).
- **DEF-2 — aria-live region not re-announced on repeat copies (identical textContent)** [src/sdlc/dashboard/static/components/resume-card/resume-card.js:98] — clicking copy a second time sets `liveRegion.textContent` to the same constant `"copied to clipboard"`; many screen readers suppress re-announcement when the value is byte-identical, so only the first copy of a session is reliably announced. **Reason deferred:** AC3's primary case (announce on copy) is satisfied; the reliable-on-repeat fix (clear-then-set on a microtask) interacts with the synchronous Playwright `inner_text` read and with SR-toggle nuances, better resolved under the dedicated a11y pass. **Action on un-defer:** clear then re-set the live region (or vary a trailing token) and add a double-copy announce test. **Owner:** Epic-5 Story 5.12 (a11y convergence gate). Surfaced by Edge Case Hunter + Acceptance Auditor (MEDIUM→a11y-hardening).
- **DEF-3 — sessionStorage property-access throw at default-param eval** [src/sdlc/dashboard/static/components/resume-card/resume-card.js:109] — `renderResumeCard(root, data, { storage = sessionStorage, ... })` evaluates the `sessionStorage` global on every call; in a sandboxed iframe without `allow-same-origin` (or full storage lockdown) the property access itself throws — outside the `try/catch` guards in `readGreetingFlag`/`markGreetingShown` — so the whole card renders blank. **Reason deferred:** the dashboard is served same-origin and is not embedded in a sandboxed iframe; the realistic storage-throws (getItem/setItem) are already guarded. **Action on un-defer:** acquire storage via a `safeStorage()` helper that try/catches the access and returns `null`, with read/mark guards no-op on `null`. **Owner:** Epic-5 component robustness (revisit if the dashboard is ever embedded). Surfaced by Edge Case Hunter (LOW).
- **DEF-4 — Long-command overflow/wrap on the inverted command surface** [src/sdlc/dashboard/static/components/inverted-command/inverted-command.css:17-28] — `.inverted-command__text` sets `flex:1 1 auto; min-width:0` but no `overflow`/`white-space`/`text-overflow`, so an unbreakable long command can overflow or awkwardly wrap inside the dark pill. **Reason deferred:** the synthetic command is short; long/real commands arrive with 5.18, and the surface is reused by 5.11 (activity feed) / 5.19 (STOP banner) which will set their own overflow policy. **Action on un-defer:** add `overflow-x:auto` (or ellipsis) and a defined `white-space` for the command text when real/long commands land. **Owner:** Epic-5 Story 5.18 / 5.11 (surface consumers). Surfaced by Blind Hunter (LOW).
- **DEF-5 — §6.4 polite live-region does not wrap breadcrumb + command for poll updates** [src/sdlc/dashboard/static/components/resume-card/resume-card.js:69-79] — `ensureLiveRegion` creates a separate sr-only region used only for the "copied to clipboard" message; the breadcrumb/command are not inside any live region, so §6.4's "announce updates after polling" is not realized. **Reason deferred:** AC3's copy announcement is satisfied; live wrapping of breadcrumb/command is a real-poll concern with no synthetic trigger in 5.8 (Acceptance Auditor confirms not an AC breach). **Action on un-defer:** wrap breadcrumb+command in an `aria-live="polite"` region when real poll-driven updates land. **Owner:** Epic-5 Story 5.18 (real poll updates). Surfaced by Acceptance Auditor (LOW).
- **DEF-6 — `.copy-btn` reset/sizing lives in resume-card.css, not the reusable inverted-command.css** [src/sdlc/dashboard/static/components/resume-card/resume-card.css:64-77] — `.inverted-command` (the reusable §7.7 class) lays out a right-edge button via `display:flex; gap`, but the `.copy-btn` chrome reset (`min-width:36px`, `border:none`, `background:transparent`, flex) lives in resume-card.css; a future surface importing only inverted-command.css gets the box but a default-chromed button. **Reason deferred:** 5.8 renders correctly; relocating `.copy-btn` ripples into the `assert "36px" in css` / `assert ".copy-btn" in css` unit assertions (which read resume-card.css only) — better decided when 5.11/5.19 actually consume the surface (YAGNI). **Action on un-defer:** move `.copy-btn` into inverted-command.css (or a shared button partial) and re-point the unit assertions when a second consumer appears. **Owner:** Epic-5 Story 5.11 / 5.19 (surface consumers). Surfaced by Acceptance Auditor (MEDIUM→forward-looking).
- **DEF-7 — Test gaps around copy/greeting boundary paths** [tests/integration/test_dashboard_resume_card.py + tests/unit/dashboard/test_resume_card_fixture.py] — uncovered: greeting on an attributed card (pairs with the story's decision-needed item), clipboard-failure path (`navigator.clipboard` undefined / `writeText` rejecting), rapid double-click race (the `clearTimeout` guard + repeat aria-live), normalizeCommand boundaries (interior newline / `null` / `>`/`❯` prefixes / empty), and sessionStorage-throws fail-safe. **Reason deferred:** these are test-strength gaps, not code defects; each pairs with a deferred behavior (5.18 real card / 5.12 a11y) and the green suite already covers the synthetic happy paths. **Action on un-defer:** add the boundary tests alongside the corresponding 5.18/5.12 behavior work. **Owner:** Epic-5 Story 5.18 / 5.12 (test hardening). Surfaced by Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter (LOW).
- **DEF-8 — Greeting burned + redundant multi-render + uncancelled timer on attributed-card upgrade** [src/sdlc/dashboard/static/components/resume-card/resume-card.js:118-124,197-201,88-107] (was the story's decision-needed item, deferred 2026-06-26) — `attributeChangedCallback` runs a full synchronous `_render` per observed attribute, and the greeting decision + `markGreetingShown` live inside the render path; a card with attributes AND storage-based greeting (no `show-greeting="false"`) upgrades with N renders where #1 shows + burns the once-per-session flag and #2+ omit it → greeting added-then-removed before paint, flag consumed unseen. Same multi-render leaves an uncancelled copy-feedback `setTimeout` / no `disconnectedCallback`. **Reason deferred:** latent — not triggered by 5.8's synthetic fixtures (the only attributed card uses `show-greeting="false"`; the greeting card has no attributes → single render), so no AC is broken and the full suite is green; the render-coalescing + lifecycle-timer fix interacts with 5.18's real rendering and with Playwright synchronous-read timing, so it belongs where the real attributed card lands. **Action on un-defer:** coalesce renders (microtask-debounced `_render` with a pending guard) so a multi-attribute upgrade renders once, lift the copy-feedback timer to the instance, and add a `disconnectedCallback` that clears it; add a test for greeting on an attributed first-session card. **Owner:** Epic-5 Story 5.18 (real Resume Card). Surfaced by Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter (HIGH-in-code / latent-in-5.8).

## Deferred from: code review of 5-11-tabs-activity-feed-empty-state-section-block-heading (2026-06-26)

> bmad-code-review, **3** adversarial layers (Blind Hunter / Edge Case Hunter / Acceptance Auditor) @ Opus-4.8 + orchestrator source-verification (every load-bearing finding reproduced against the real `tabs.js` / `activity-feed.js` / `empty-state.js` / `section-heading.js` / fixtures / unit + Playwright tests). Story 5.11 reviewed solo (only story in `review`, uncommitted working tree on `main`). Acceptance Auditor: **AC1 MET, AC2 PARTIAL** (HIGH feed-ordering defect, patched), **AC3 MET, AC4 MET**; D1–D5 as resolved (a); no anti-scope-creep; no XSS. Triage: **0 decision-needed + 4 patch (story Review Findings), 8 defer (below), 2 dismissed**. The HIGH (`activity-feed.js` renders oldest-on-top and evicts the *newest* entry) was independently surfaced by ALL THREE layers and shipped green because the only feed test was a source-substring grep. Dismissed: Playwright `!= "body"` assertion redundant-but-harmless (real focus-drop guard is `assert active`); duplicated Change Log block in the story doc (cosmetic).

- **DEF-1 — Shared module-singleton mutation across instances (immutability + multi-instance state leak)** [src/sdlc/dashboard/static/components/tabs/tabs.js:86-89; src/sdlc/dashboard/static/components/activity-feed/activity-feed.js:132-138] — `activateTab` does `data.activeTabId = tabKey` and `prependActivityFeedEntry` does `data.entries = …`, where `data` defaults to the exported `SYNTHETIC_*_FIXTURE` singleton (via `host._fixtureRef`). Two `<dashboard-tabs>` (or two `<activity-feed>`) on one page share + overwrite each other's state, and it violates the project immutability rule. **Reason deferred:** latent — the committed fixtures mount a single instance of each; a proper fix is a per-host state store (clone-on-write vs per-instance store is a design choice), better decided when real multi-instance reuse lands. **Action on un-defer:** give each host its own state object (don't default-mutate the shared singleton) and treat updates immutably. **Owner:** Epic-5 Story 5.16 (real agent-runs render). Surfaced by Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter (MEDIUM→latent).
- **DEF-2 — Missing-`id` feed entry duplicates on every poll** [src/sdlc/dashboard/static/components/activity-feed/activity-feed.js:69,114-119] — `row.dataset.entryId = entry.id` stores `undefined` as the string `"undefined"`, but the dedupe set is checked with `existingIds.has(entry.id)` (the value `undefined`); a real entry lacking an id re-inserts on every poll → unbounded duplicate rows. **Reason deferred:** synthetic data always carries ids; real `agent_runs.jsonl` rows are read in 5.16, which owns the source swap of this render seam. **Action on un-defer:** key by `entry.id ?? \`row-${index}\`` consistently on both the `dataset` write and the `Set` check. **Owner:** Epic-5 Story 5.16. Surfaced by Edge Case Hunter (MEDIUM→5.16-seam).
- **DEF-3 — Unknown outcome silently renders the `error` glyph + "Error" label** [src/sdlc/dashboard/static/components/activity-feed/activity-feed.js:42-43] — `OUTCOME_GLYPH[outcome] || OUTCOME_GLYPH.error` maps any value outside `{approved,rejected,error}` (e.g. real `running`/`timeout`/`skipped`) to the red error glyph + "Error", mislabeling an in-progress run as a failure. **Reason deferred:** synthetic data uses only the three known outcomes; the unknown-outcome space appears with real data in 5.16. **Action on un-defer:** add a neutral/in-progress glyph+label mapping (or an explicit fallback) when real outcomes land. **Owner:** Epic-5 Story 5.16. Surfaced by Edge Case Hunter (LOW).
- **DEF-4 — Missing feed field renders the literal string "undefined"** [src/sdlc/dashboard/static/components/activity-feed/activity-feed.js:71-85] — `textContent = entry.timestamp` (and agent/target/duration) coerces a missing field to `"undefined"` in the cell. **Reason deferred:** synthetic data always populates all 5 fields; real rows (5.16) may omit one. **Action on un-defer:** guard each field with a fallback (`entry.timestamp ?? "—"`) when real data lands. **Owner:** Epic-5 Story 5.16. Surfaced by Edge Case Hunter (LOW).
- **DEF-5 — `renderEmptyState({message:""})` blanks the anti-cynicism message on the function path** [src/sdlc/dashboard/static/components/empty-state/empty-state.js:12] — the `{ message = EMPTY_STATE_MESSAGE }` default only fires for `undefined`, so an explicit `""` from a direct caller renders a blank `<p>` (the footer still renders, so not fully blank, but the UX-DR15 copy is gone). The custom-element path is guarded (`getAttribute("message") || EMPTY_STATE_MESSAGE`). **Reason deferred:** no current caller passes `""`; the empty-state's first external consumer is 5.19 (STOP banner column). **Action on un-defer:** coerce falsy `message` to `EMPTY_STATE_MESSAGE` inside `renderEmptyState`. **Owner:** Epic-5 Story 5.19. Surfaced by Edge Case Hunter (LOW).
- **DEF-6 — `renderSectionBlockHeading({count:0})` blanks a numeric-0 count** [src/sdlc/dashboard/static/components/section-heading/section-heading.js:17] — `count || ""` turns a numeric `0` into an empty count cell ("0 stories" disappears). The element path is safe (attributes are non-empty strings like "0 active"); only a raw numeric-`0` function call blanks. **Reason deferred:** real numeric counts arrive when sections render live data (5.14/5.15); today all callers pass strings. **Action on un-defer:** use `count == null ? "" : String(count)`. **Owner:** Epic-5 Story 5.14 / 5.15. Surfaced by Edge Case Hunter (LOW).
- **DEF-7 — No standalone `section-heading.fixture.html` (D4 wording said "+ .fixture.html")** [src/sdlc/dashboard/static/components/section-heading/] — the section-block-heading element is exercised only inside `editorial-scanning-rhythm.html`; D4's recommendation named a dedicated `.fixture.html`. Non-AC-blocking (AC4 needs no standalone fixture). **Reason deferred:** cosmetic/deliverable-wording gap; the element is fully exercised via the rhythm fixture + tests. **Action on un-defer:** add `section-heading.fixture.html` (+ force-include) for parity with the other components. **Owner:** Epic-5 component-convention tidy. Surfaced by Acceptance Auditor (LOW).
- **DEF-8 — Remaining unit "contract" tests are substring greps, not DOM contracts** [tests/unit/dashboard/test_tabs_activity_feed_fixture.py:45-76,109-113] — `test_tabs_fixture_has_tablist_tab_tabpanel_contract`, `test_activity_feed_entry_has_five_fields`, and `test_section_heading_js_exports_renderer` only assert that strings (`role="tab"`, `aria-controls`, field names, `display-3`) appear *somewhere* in the JS source; none verifies rendered output or that `aria-controls` resolves to a real panel. **Reason deferred:** AC1 IS behaviorally covered by the 5 real Playwright tabs tests (incl. Enter-reveals-the-aria-controls-panel), so this is test-rigor, not a coverage hole; the feed-specific greps are addressed by the patched behavioral feed test. **Action on un-defer:** promote the residual markup/field greps to executing DOM assertions during the 5.12 a11y convergence pass. **Owner:** Epic-5 Story 5.12 (a11y convergence gate). Surfaced by Blind Hunter + Acceptance Auditor (LOW).

Order is only partially covered (Tabs ArrowRight/Home/End + backlog-tree ArrowDown). **Reason deferred:** AC3's reachability + focus-visibility sub-criteria are the load-bearing ones (and are patched); a full §8.4 sequence contract over the composite surface is non-trivial and better authored against the real assembled SPA. **Action on un-defer:** assert the ordered Tab sequence (and intra-widget arrow sequence) against the §8.4 per-component checklist when full page assembly lands. **Owner:** Epic-5 Story 5.14–5.18 (real SPA assembly) / 5.22 (release a11y gate). ## Deferred from: code review of 5-12-forbidden-patterns-enforcement-wcag-2-2-level-a-baseline (2026-07-01, fresh-context re-review)

> bmad-code-review fresh-context RE-review of the **committed** branch (`main...HEAD`, 22 files / +983−2), 3 adversarial layers (Blind Hunter / Edge Case Hunter / Acceptance Auditor) @ Opus-4.8 + orchestrator source-verification (fixture-resolution failure reproduced with a stdlib pytest repro → `fixture 'myfix' not found`; off-by-7 column + inline-`<script>`/`<style>` HTML bypass + `data-toast-card`/`shimmering-*` false-positives all reproduced against the real scanner; CSP-block dismissed after confirming `server.py` sends no CSP header). Triage: **1 decision-needed + 3 patch (story Review Findings 2026-07-01) + 7 defer (below) + 6 dismissed**. Headline: the a11y harness fixture `dashboard_composite_url` is undiscoverable → 9 `@pytest.mark.integration` tests ERROR on CI (the prior review missed this — it patched test logic but never ran pytest collection/setup). The 3 patches (P1 fixture→conftest, P2 off-by-7 column, P3 data-toast false-positive) live in the story Review Findings; the decision D1 (scanner document/quote-aware hardening vs ratify+defer) awaits resolution.

- **DEF-A — a11y suite silently skips on any Chromium launch failure → false-green HARD gate** [tests/dashboard/_playwright_a11y.py:71] — `with_playwright_page` does `except PlaywrightError: pytest.skip(...)`, swallowing ANY Chromium launch failure (missing OS lib despite `--with-deps`, sandbox/seccomp denial), not just "not installed"; `uv run pytest` then exits 0 with AC2/AC3/AC4 unverified, and there is no distinct "a11y-actually-ran" required check (the adopt suite has `posix-adopt-ran` precisely because an all-skipped run is a false green). **Reason deferred:** the chromium-skip-guard is the ratified posture (5.10 DEF-1), and this is only reachable AFTER P1 makes the fixture resolve. **Action on un-defer:** narrow the `except` to a genuine "executable not found" (re-raise other `PlaywrightError`s so the test ERRORs), or add a required CI check asserting the a11y tests actually executed (non-skipped) on the Linux cell. **Owner:** dashboard a11y CI hardening / 5.22. Surfaced by Edge Case Hunter (MEDIUM).
- **DEF-B — Fail-open: no-arg scan + missing `_DEFAULT_ROOT` returns exit 0 "gate OK"** [scripts/check_dashboard_forbidden_patterns.py:88-90] — `_expand_targets` returns `([], [])` when `not root.is_dir()`; `main` then prints "gate OK (no §7.12 violations)" and returns 0. CI/pre-commit invoke the gate with no args, so relocating/renaming `src/sdlc/dashboard/static` silently disables the release-blocking check with zero signal. **Reason deferred:** identical idiom in the sibling `check_dashboard_color_only.py` (prior-dismissed as a shared gate idiom); fixing one without the other is inconsistent. **Action on un-defer:** exit ≥1 (or a dedicated "target-missing" code) when the no-arg default root is absent, applied to both dashboard gates repo-wide. **Owner:** dashboard gate hardening (repo-wide). Surfaced by Edge Case Hunter + Blind Hunter (MEDIUM→LOW).
- **DEF-C — Server thread + bound port leak on the readiness-timeout path** [tests/dashboard/_playwright_a11y.py:44-60] — the `dashboard_composite_url` fixture's `while … else: pytest.fail("dashboard server did not become ready")` fires before `yield`, so `server.shutdown()`/`server.server_close()`/`thread.join()` never run. **Reason deferred:** error-path only (server always ready within 5s), and identical to `tests/dashboard/conftest.py::running_dashboard` (this is the prior review's DEF-1, still open). **Action on un-defer:** when P1 moves this fixture into conftest.py, wrap startup in try/finally so teardown runs on readiness timeout, and apply the same fix to the sibling `running_dashboard`. **Owner:** dashboard test-fixture hardening (repo-wide; do with P1). Surfaced by Edge Case Hunter + Blind Hunter (LOW).
- **DEF-D — `find_free_port` → `create_server` bind is a TOCTOU race** [src/sdlc/dashboard/server.py:262-266] — `find_free_port` binds port 0, reads the number, closes the probe socket, and returns; another process can grab that ephemeral port before `create_server` binds it (busy CI runner, parallel fixtures), raising `OSError` in fixture setup → test ERROR (flake), not a graceful retry. **Reason deferred:** pre-existing shared idiom used by every dashboard server fixture; low incidence. **Action on un-defer:** retry `find_free_port`/`create_server` on bind `OSError`, or hand the pre-bound socket to the server. **Owner:** dashboard server test-infra (repo-wide). Surfaced by Edge Case Hunter (LOW).
- **DEF-E — Skeleton/shimmer detection is substring- not token-aware (docstring overstates "token-aware")** [scripts/check_dashboard_forbidden_patterns.py:33-35] — `_SKELETON_HINT = "(?:skeleton|shimmer|placeholder-loading)"` has no boundary, so `.search()` matches `shimmer` inside `shimmering-headline` / `.shimmering-text` and flags a release-blocking violation on a non-skeleton class. **Reason deferred:** near-zero real risk in this anti-motion repo (no shimmer classes exist; scanner exits 0 on the real tree), and a token-safe fix must still allow the intended BEM `skeleton__row` / compound `loading-skeleton` matches (the reason boundaries were dropped). **Action on un-defer:** match the hint as a token allowing `-`/`__` joins but not a plain word continuation (`shimmer` yes, `shimmering` no). **Owner:** scanner precision (with D1 hardening). Surfaced by Blind Hunter (MEDIUM→LOW).
- **DEF-F — Skeleton false-negative: `@keyframes shimmer` / `animation:` (no leading `.`) + JS `classList.add('skeleton')`** [scripts/check_dashboard_forbidden_patterns.py:47-54] — the CSS matcher requires a leading `.` (class selector) and the HTML matcher reads only `class="…"` attributes, so a keyframed shimmer loader (`@keyframes shimmer{…}` + `animation: shimmer 1s`) and a JS-applied class evade the gate. **Reason deferred:** the `@keyframes`/`animation` path is plausibly already caught by the DD-14 motion gate (which forbids non-pulse keyframes/transitions) — verify before adding a redundant rule; the JS-`classList` path is the existing DEF-3 (JS-authored tokens, owned by 5.22). **Action on un-defer:** confirm DD-14 coverage of shimmer keyframes; if not covered, add an `@keyframes`/`animation`-name skeleton rule. **Owner:** DD-14 motion gate reconcile / 5.22. Surfaced by Blind Hunter (LOW).
- **DEF-G — New `activity-feed__list` `tabindex="0"` has no `:focus-visible` ring assertion** [src/sdlc/dashboard/static/components/activity-feed/activity-feed.js + tests/dashboard/test_keyboard_only.py:56] — the AC2 fix makes the scroll region keyboard-focusable (axe `scrollable-region-focusable`, Level-A 2.1.1), creating a new Tab stop; the keyboard harness asserts a DD-15 ring only for `resume-card .copy-btn`, so if the list has no `:focus-visible` ring a keyboard user lands on invisible focus (AC3 "focus always visible", SC 2.4.7 = Level AA, reported-not-blocking here). **Reason deferred:** AA-level (not gate-blocking), and better asserted against the real assembled SPA. **Action on un-defer:** add a focus-ring assertion for the focusable feed list (and a `:focus-visible` ring if missing) alongside the §8.4 focus-order work (DEF-2). **Owner:** Epic-5 SPA assembly (5.14–5.18) / 5.22. Surfaced by Blind Hunter (MEDIUM→LOW/AA).
